\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00315}00315   uint64\_t a = lhs >> 32, b = lhs \& \mbox{\hyperlink{structmask}{mask}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00316}00316   uint64\_t c = rhs >> 32, d = rhs \& \mbox{\hyperlink{structmask}{mask}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00317}00317   uint64\_t ac = a * c, bc = b * c, ad = a * d, bd = b * d;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00318}00318   \textcolor{comment}{// Compute mid 64-\/bit of result and round.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00319}00319   uint64\_t mid = (bd >> 32) + (ad \& \mbox{\hyperlink{structmask}{mask}}) + (bc \& \mbox{\hyperlink{structmask}{mask}}) + (1U << 31);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l00320}00320   \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} ac + (ad >> 32) + (bc >> 32) + (mid >> 32);}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01808}01808     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} compression\_ratio = 27;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01809}01809 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01810}01810     \textcolor{comment}{// Compute base index.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01811}01811     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} cache\_index = (k -\/ float\_info<double>::min\_k) / compression\_ratio;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01812}01812     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} kb = cache\_index * compression\_ratio + float\_info<double>::min\_k;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01813}01813     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} offset = k -\/ kb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01814}01814 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01817}01817     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (offset == 0) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} base\_cache;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01818}01818 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01819}01819     \textcolor{comment}{// Compute the required amount of bit-\/shift.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01820}01820     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} alpha = floor\_log2\_pow10(kb + offset) -\/ floor\_log2\_pow10(kb) -\/ offset;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01821}01821     FMT\_ASSERT(alpha > 0 \&\& alpha < 64, \textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}shifting error detected"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01822}01822 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01823}01823     \textcolor{comment}{// Try to recover the real cache.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01824}01824     uint64\_t pow5 = powers\_of\_5\_64[offset];}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01825}01825     \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1uint128__wrapper}{uint128\_wrapper}} recovered\_cache = umul128(base\_cache.high(), pow5);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01826}01826     \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1uint128__wrapper}{uint128\_wrapper}} middle\_low =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01827}01827         umul128(base\_cache.low() -\/ (kb < 0 ? 1u : 0u), pow5);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01828}01828 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01829}01829     recovered\_cache += middle\_low.high();}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01830}01830 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01831}01831     uint64\_t high\_to\_middle = recovered\_cache.high() << (64 -\/ alpha);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01832}01832     uint64\_t middle\_to\_low = recovered\_cache.low() << (64 -\/ alpha);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01833}01833 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01834}01834     recovered\_cache =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01835}01835         \mbox{\hyperlink{structdetail_1_1uint128__wrapper}{uint128\_wrapper}}\{(recovered\_cache.low() >> alpha) | high\_to\_middle,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01836}01836                         ((middle\_low.low() >> alpha) | middle\_to\_low)\};}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01837}01837 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01838}01838     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (kb < 0) recovered\_cache += 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01839}01839 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01840}01840     \textcolor{comment}{// Get error.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01842}01842     uint32\_t error = (pow10\_recovery\_errors[error\_idx] >>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01843}01843                       ((k -\/ float\_info<double>::min\_k) \% 16) * 2) \&}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01844}01844                      0x3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01845}01845 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01846}01846     \textcolor{comment}{// Add the error back.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l01848}01848     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} \{recovered\_cache.high(), recovered\_cache.low() + error\};}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l02222}02222 \textcolor{comment}{// Formats a floating-\/point number using a variation of the Fixed-\/Precision}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{format-inl_8h_source_l02225}02225 FMT\_CONSTEXPR20 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} \textcolor{keywordtype}{void} format\_dragon(fp \mbox{\hyperlink{classvalue}{value}}, \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool} is\_predecessor\_closer,}
